# Initialize Chat | v0 Docs

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Chats

Initialize Chat
===============

Copy page

Initializes a new chat from source content such as files, repositories, registries, or zip archives. Enables context-rich conversations based on code or assets.

POST/v1/chats/init

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/init#usage)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

FilesRepositoryRegistryZIP Archive

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: [\
        {\
          name: 'app/globals.css',\
          content: `\
            body {\
              background-color: black;\
              color: white;\
            }\
          `,\
        },\
      ],
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/init#api-signature)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/init#request)

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/init#body)

name?: string

A user-defined name for the chat. Helps identify or describe the purpose of the chat session in the UI or API responses.

chatPrivacy?: 'public' | 'private' | 'team-edit' | 'team' | 'unlisted'

Controls the visibility of the chat. Defines whether the chat is private, shared with a team, or publicly accessible.

projectId?: string

Associates the chat with a specific project. Useful for organizing and grouping chats in a workspace.

type?: 'template'

Specifies the initialization method. For this endpoint, it defines the source of content being used to initialize the chat.

files?: object | object\[\]

An array of inline file objects used to initialize the chat. Each object must contain a file `name` and its `content`.

name?: string

url?: string

locked?: boolean

Whether to lock this file to prevent AI from overwriting it during generation

content?: string

repo?: object

Specifies a repository source for initialization. Supports both public and private GitHub repositories. For private repositories, ensure your GitHub account is connected through Vercel.

url: string

branch?: string

lockAllFiles?: boolean

Whether to lock all files from the zip archive to prevent AI from overwriting them during generation

registry?: object

Allows initialization from a predefined component or code registry. Includes the registry source and identifier for the desired component/module.

url: string

zip?: object

Provides a zipped bundle of files as the input source. Typically includes a base64-encoded archive or a remote URL reference.

url: string

templateId?: string

The ID of the template to initialize the chat from. This should be a valid template ID from the v0 template system.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/init#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the chat.

object: 'chat'

Fixed value identifying this object as a chat.

shareable: boolean

Indicates whether the chat can be shared via public link.

privacy: 'public' | 'private' | 'team' | 'team-edit' | 'unlisted'

Defines the visibility of the chat—private, team-only, or public.

name?: string

An optional name assigned to the chat by the user.

title?: string

deprecated

Deprecated title field preserved for backward compatibility.

createdAt: string

The ISO timestamp representing when the chat was created.

updatedAt?: string

The ISO timestamp of the last update to the chat.

favorite: boolean

Indicates whether the chat is marked as a favorite.

authorId: string

The ID of the user who created the chat.

projectId?: string

Optional ID of the v0 project associated with this chat.

webUrl: string

Web URL to view this chat in the browser.

apiUrl: string

API URL to access this chat via the API.

latestVersion?: object

Full details of the most recent generated version, if available.

id: string

A unique identifier for the version.

object: 'version'

Fixed value identifying this object as a version.

status: 'pending' | 'completed' | 'failed'

The current status of the version generation process.

demoUrl?: string

Optional URL for previewing the generated output.

screenshotUrl?: string

URL to retrieve a screenshot of this version.

createdAt: string

The date and time when the version was created, in ISO 8601 format.

updatedAt?: string

The date and time when the version was last updated, in ISO 8601 format.

files: object\[\]

A list of files that were generated or included in this version.

url: string

deprecated

The canonical URL to access this chat.

messages: object\[\]

All messages exchanged in the chat, including user and assistant entries.

id: string

A unique identifier for the message.

object: 'message'

Fixed value identifying this object as a message.

content: string

The main text content of the message.

experimental\_content?: any\[\] | any\[\]\[\]

The parsed content of the message as an array structure containing AST nodes. This is an experimental field that may change.

createdAt: string

The ISO timestamp representing when the message was created.

updatedAt?: string

The ISO timestamp representing when the message was last updated.

type: 'message' | 'forked-block' | 'forked-chat' | 'open-in-v0' | 'refinement' | 'added-environment-variables' | 'added-integration' | 'deleted-file' | 'moved-file' | 'renamed-file' | 'edited-file' | 'replace-src' | 'reverted-block' | 'fix-with-v0' | 'auto-fix-with-v0' | 'sync-git' | 'fix-cve' | 'answered-questions'

Indicates the format or category of the message, such as plain text or code.

role: 'user' | 'assistant'

Specifies whether the message was sent by the user or the assistant.

finishReason?: 'stop' | 'length' | 'content-filter' | 'tool-calls' | 'error' | 'other' | 'unknown'

The reason why the message generation finished.

apiUrl: string

API URL to access this message via the API.

authorId: stringnull

The ID of the user who sent the message.

parentId?: stringnull

The ID of the parent message.

attachments?: object\[\]

url: string

The URL where the attachment file can be accessed.

name?: string

The original filename of the attachment.

contentType?: string

The MIME type of the attachment file (e.g., image/png, application/pdf).

size: number

The size of the attachment file in bytes.

content?: string

The base64-encoded content of the attachment file, if available.

type?: 'screenshot' | 'figma' | 'zip'

Optional v0-specific attachment type for enhanced processing.

files?: object\[\]

Optional array of files associated with the chat context.

lang: string

Programming language used in the file (e.g., JavaScript, Python).

meta: object

A key-value map of metadata associated with the file (e.g., path, type).

source: string

The origin or identifier of the file source (e.g., path or upload label).

demo?: string

deprecated

Deprecated demo URL used for previewing the chat result.

text: string

The main user prompt or instruction that started the chat.

modelConfiguration?: object

The configuration used to generate responses in this chat.

modelId?: 'v0-mini' | 'v0-pro' | 'v0-max'

deprecated

Deprecated Model ID field preserved for backward compatibility.

imageGenerations?: boolean

Enables image generations to generate up to 5 images per version.

thinking?: boolean

Enables thinking to generate a response in multiple steps.

permissions: object

write: boolean

If true, the user has write access to the chat.

[Find Chats\
\
Retrieves a list of existing chats, with support for pagination and filtering by favorite status. Helps manage and navigate chat history.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/find)
[Delete Chat\
\
Deletes a specific chat based on the provided chatId. This operation is irreversible and permanently removes the chat and its contents.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/delete)

v0 Platform API/Guides

Start from Existing Code
========================

Copy page

Learn how to start v0 chats from existing codebases, repositories, and file structures

Learn how to bootstrap v0 chats from your existing code, whether it's a GitHub repository, local files, or zip archives.

[Overview](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#overview)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The v0 Platform API supports multiple ways to initialize chats from existing code:

*   **GitHub Repositories** - Import directly from public or private repos
*   **File Uploads** - Upload individual files with content
*   **Zip Archives** - Import from zip file URLs
*   **Registry Components** - Use community components

[Importing from GitHub Repositories](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#importing-from-github-repositories)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Basic Repository Import](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#basic-repository-import)

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    // Initialize chat from GitHub repository
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'repo',
      repo: {
        url: 'https://github.com/username/my-react-app',
        branch: 'main', // optional, defaults to default branch
      },
      projectId: 'your-project-id', // optional
      name: 'My Imported Project', // optional
    })
    
    console.log(`Chat created: ${chat.id}`)

### [Lock Files from Modification](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#lock-files-from-modification)

    // Initialize with all files locked to prevent AI modification
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'repo',
      repo: {
        url: 'https://github.com/username/my-app',
      },
      lockAllFiles: true, // Prevents AI from modifying any files
    })

[Importing from Files](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#importing-from-files)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Upload Individual Files](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#upload-individual-files)

    // Initialize chat with specific files
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: [\
        {\
          name: 'src/components/Button.tsx',\
          content: `\
            import React from 'react'\
    \
            export function Button({ children, onClick }) {\
              return (\
                <button onClick={onClick} className="btn">\
                  {children}\
                </button>\
              )\
            }\
          `,\
          locked: false, // Allow AI to modify this file\
        },\
        {\
          name: 'src/styles/button.css',\
          content: `\
            .btn {\
              padding: 8px 16px;\
              border: none;\
              border-radius: 4px;\
              background: #007bff;\
              color: white;\
              cursor: pointer;\
            }\
          `,\
          locked: true, // Prevent AI from modifying this file\
        },\
      ],
    })

### [Upload from URLs](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#upload-from-urls)

    // Initialize chat with files from URLs
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: [\
        {\
          name: 'package.json',\
          url: 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/username/repo/main/package.json',\
        },\
        {\
          name: 'README.md',\
          url: 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/username/repo/main/README.md',\
          locked: true,\
        },\
      ],
    })

[Importing from Zip Archives](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#importing-from-zip-archives)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // Initialize chat from zip file URL
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'zip',
      zip: {
        url: 'https://github.com/username/project/archive/refs/heads/main.zip',
      },
      lockAllFiles: false, // Allow AI to modify files
      name: 'Project from Archive',
    })

[Importing from Community Registries](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#importing-from-community-registries)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For specialized use cases, you can import from component registries:

    // Initialize chat from component registry (e.g., shadcn/ui)
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'registry',
      registry: {
        url: 'https://ui.shadcn.com/registry/styles/default/button.json',
      },
      lockAllFiles: false,
    })

[Working with Projects](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#working-with-projects)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Create Project and Chat Together](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#create-project-and-chat-together)

    // Create a project first
    const project = await v0.projects.create({
      name: 'My React App',
      description: 'Imported React application',
      environmentVariables: [\
        { key: 'NODE_ENV', value: 'development' },\
        { key: 'API_URL', value: 'http://localhost:3001' },\
      ],
    })
    
    // Then initialize chat with the project
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'repo',
      repo: {
        url: 'https://github.com/username/react-app',
      },
      projectId: project.id,
      name: 'Development Chat',
    })

[Chat vs Init vs Create](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#chat-vs-init-vs-create)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [When to Use `chats.init()`](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#when-to-use-chatsinit)

Use `chats.init()` when you have existing code and want to start development:

*   **Fast** - No AI processing during initialization
*   **Free** - Doesn't consume tokens
*   **Files-first** - Start with existing code structure

### [When to Use `chats.create()`](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#when-to-use-chatscreate)

Use `chats.create()` when starting from scratch:

*   **AI-powered** - Generates initial code from prompts
*   **Token cost** - Consumes tokens for AI generation
*   **Prompt-first** - Start with natural language description

    // chats.init() - Fast, no tokens, existing code
    const initChat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: existingFiles,
    })
    
    // chats.create() - Slower, uses tokens, generates code
    const createChat = await v0.chats.create({
      message: 'Create a React dashboard with charts',
    })

[Best Practices](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#best-practices)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [1\. File Organization](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#1-file-organization)

    // ✅ Good: Organized file structure
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: [\
        { name: 'src/components/Button.tsx', content: '...' },\
        { name: 'src/components/Card.tsx', content: '...' },\
        { name: 'src/styles/globals.css', content: '...' },\
        { name: 'package.json', content: '...', locked: true },\
      ],
    })

### [2\. Selective File Locking](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#2-selective-file-locking)

    // ✅ Good: Lock configuration files, allow code modification
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'files',
      files: [\
        { name: 'src/App.tsx', content: '...', locked: false }, // Allow AI changes\
        { name: 'package.json', content: '...', locked: true }, // Protect config\
        { name: '.env.example', content: '...', locked: true }, // Protect secrets\
      ],
    })

### [3\. Project Integration](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/start-from-existing-code#3-project-integration)

    // ✅ Good: Use projects for organization
    const project = await v0.projects.create({
      name: 'Frontend Components',
      instructions: 'Focus on accessible, reusable React components',
    })
    
    const chat = await v0.chats.init({
      type: 'repo',
      repo: { url: 'https://github.com/company/ui-library' },
      projectId: project.id,
    })

[Displaying Chat Messages\
\
Learn how to render and format chat messages from the v0 Platform API using @v0-sdk/react](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/displaying-chat-messages)
[Environment Variables\
\
Learn how to manage environment variables and configuration in v0 projects](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/guides/environment-variables)

Menu

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Hooks

Find Hooks
==========

Copy page

Retrieves a list of existing hooks in your workspace. Useful for managing active webhooks tied to chat events or deployments.

GET/v1/hooks

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/find#usage)

---------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.hooks.find()
    
    console.log(result)

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/find#response)

object: 'list'

data: object\[\]

id?: string

A unique identifier for the webhook.

object?: 'hook'

Fixed value identifying this object as a webhook.

name?: string

A user-defined name to label the webhook.

[Find Vercel Projects\
\
Retrieves a list of Vercel projects linked to your integration. Useful for associating chats, deployments, or hooks with specific Vercel projects.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.find)
[Create Hook\
\
Creates a new webhook that listens for specific events. Supports optional association with a chat.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create)

Menu

Agentic Features
================

Copy page

v0's intelligent agent capabilities for web search, site inspection, and error fixing.

v0 is an intelligent agent that can autonomously perform complex tasks beyond just generating code. The agent system combines web search, site inspection, error fixing, and external tool integration to create a truly autonomous development assistant.

[Core Agent Capabilities](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#core-agent-capabilities)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Web Search](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#web-search)

v0 can search the web in real-time and provide cited results directly in your chat.

**Features:**

*   Real-time web search with citation tracking
*   Rich result display with clickable source links
*   Progressive UI states showing search progress
*   Animated loading indicators

**How it works:** When you ask v0 to search for current information, the SearchWeb subagent automatically queries the web, analyzes results, and presents them with proper citations. Results are displayed with citation pills that link directly to the source websites.

### [Site Inspection](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#site-inspection)

v0 can visit and analyze any website, capturing screenshots and extracting content.

**Features:**

*   Automated website screenshot capture
*   Visual analysis and content extraction
*   Error handling for inaccessible sites
*   Screenshot storage and display

**Use cases:**

*   Analyzing competitor websites for design inspiration
*   Understanding the structure of existing sites
*   Capturing visual references for recreation
*   Inspecting responsive design implementations

### [Automatic Error Fixing](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#automatic-error-fixing)

v0's advanced autofix system can detect and repair various types of errors in your code.

**Types of errors it fixes:**

*   Missing files and dependencies
*   Code syntax and formatting issues
*   Runtime errors and bugs
*   Import and export problems

**How it helps:**

*   Saves time by automatically fixing common errors
*   Learns from your codebase to suggest appropriate fixes
*   Handles routine maintenance tasks so you can focus on building

[External Tool Integration](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#external-tool-integration)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Third-Party Integrations](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#third-party-integrations)

v0 can connect to external services and tools to extend its capabilities via the [Vercel Marketplace](https://vercel.com/marketplace)
.

[How Agent Capabilities Work](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#how-agent-capabilities-work)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

v0's agent system works seamlessly in the background to help you accomplish complex tasks. When you ask v0 to perform actions that require external information or tools, it automatically:

*   **Coordinates multiple tasks**: Handles complex workflows involving multiple steps
*   **Maintains context**: Remembers previous actions and results throughout the conversation
*   **Provides real-time feedback**: Shows you what it's doing as it works
*   **Handles errors gracefully**: Recovers from issues and tries alternative approaches

[User Interface](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#user-interface)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Real-time Feedback](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#real-time-feedback)

The agent system provides rich visual feedback:

*   **Progress indicators**: Live updates on agent actions
*   **Task cards**: Visual representation of ongoing tasks
*   **Citation display**: Rich formatting for web search results
*   **Tool execution**: Status cards for external tool operations

### [Agent Control](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#agent-control)

Users have full control over agent execution:

*   **Manual stops**: Interrupt agent execution at any time
*   **Auto-continue**: Automatic progression through multi-step tasks
*   **Task visibility**: Clear visibility into agent decision-making

[Getting Started](https://v0.app/docs/agentic-features#getting-started)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use v0's agent capabilities, simply ask v0 to perform tasks that require these features:

*   **"Search for the latest React best practices"** - triggers web search
*   **"Show me what GitHub's homepage looks like"** - captures a screenshot
*   **"Fix the TypeScript errors in my code"** - runs automatic error fixing
*   **"Connect to my Supabase database"** - sets up external integrations

v0 will automatically use the appropriate capabilities based on what you're asking for, with clear visual feedback showing what it's doing.

[Get started with v0](https://v0.app/docs/quickstart)

[What is v0?\
\
v0 is an AI-powered development platform that turns ideas into production-ready, full-stack web apps.](https://v0.app/docs/introduction)
[Vercel Integration\
\
How v0 and Vercel work in tandem.](https://v0.app/docs/vercel-integration)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Hooks

Create Hook
===========

Copy page

Creates a new webhook that listens for specific events. Supports optional association with a chat.

POST/v1/hooks

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.hooks.create({
      name: 'My Hook',
      events: ['chat.created', 'message.created'],
      url: 'https://example.com',
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create#request)

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create#body)

name: string

A human-readable name for the hook.

events: 'chat.created' | 'chat.updated' | 'chat.deleted' | 'message.created' | 'message.updated' | 'message.deleted' | 'message.finished'\[\]

List of event types the hook should subscribe to.

chatId?: string

The ID of a chat to scope the hook to.

url: string

The target URL to receive the webhook payloads.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the webhook.

object: 'hook'

Fixed value identifying this object as a webhook.

name: string

A user-defined name to label the webhook.

events: 'chat.created' | 'chat.updated' | 'chat.deleted' | 'message.created' | 'message.updated' | 'message.deleted' | 'message.finished'\[\]

List of event types this webhook is subscribed to.

chatId?: string

Optional ID of the chat that this webhook is scoped to.

url: string

Target URL that receives event payloads for this webhook.

[Find Hooks\
\
Retrieves a list of existing hooks in your workspace. Useful for managing active webhooks tied to chat events or deployments.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/find)
[Get Hook\
\
Retrieves the details of a specific webhook using its ID.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id)

---

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Hooks

Get Hook
========

Copy page

Retrieves the details of a specific webhook using its ID.

GET/v1/hooks/{hookId}

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id#usage)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.hooks.getById({
      hookId: '123',
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id#api-signature)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id#path-parameters)

hookId: string

The unique identifier of the hook to retrieve.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the webhook.

object: 'hook'

Fixed value identifying this object as a webhook.

name: string

A user-defined name to label the webhook.

events: 'chat.created' | 'chat.updated' | 'chat.deleted' | 'message.created' | 'message.updated' | 'message.deleted' | 'message.finished'\[\]

List of event types this webhook is subscribed to.

chatId?: string

Optional ID of the chat that this webhook is scoped to.

url: string

Target URL that receives event payloads for this webhook.

[Create Hook\
\
Creates a new webhook that listens for specific events. Supports optional association with a chat.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/create)
[Update Hook\
\
Updates the configuration of an existing webhook, including its name, event subscriptions, or target URL.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Integrations

Create Vercel Project
=====================

Copy page

Links a Vercel project to an existing v0 project. Enables Vercel-related features and deployment integration within the v0 workspace.

POST/v1/integrations/vercel/projects

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.integrations.vercel.projects.create()
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create#request)

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create#body)

projectId: string

The ID of the v0 project to link to the new Vercel project.

name: string

The name to assign to the new Vercel project.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the linked Vercel project.

object: 'vercel\_project'

Fixed value identifying this object as a Vercel project.

name: string

The name of the Vercel project.

[Find Deployment Errors\
\
Retrieves a list of errors that occurred during a specific deployment. Useful for diagnosing and debugging deployment issues.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/deployments/find-errors)
[Find Vercel Projects\
\
Retrieves a list of Vercel projects linked to your integration. Useful for associating chats, deployments, or hooks with specific Vercel projects.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.find)

v0 Platform API/Packages

@v0-sdk/react
=============

Copy page

Headless React components for rendering v0 Platform API content

Headless React components for rendering content from the v0 Platform API. Provides components for streaming messages, code blocks, thinking sections, and more.

[Installation](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#installation)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    npm install @v0-sdk/react
    # or
    pnpm add @v0-sdk/react
    # or
    yarn add @v0-sdk/react

[Quick Start](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#quick-start)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    import { StreamingMessage } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function ChatInterface({ message }) {
      return (
        <StreamingMessage
          message={message}
          onComplete={(result) => {
            console.log('Streaming complete:', result)
          }}
        />
      )
    }

[Components](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#components)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [StreamingMessage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#streamingmessage)

Renders streaming chat messages with real-time updates.

    import { StreamingMessage } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function Chat() {
      return (
        <StreamingMessage
          message={streamingData}
          theme="elegant"
          className="my-message"
          onComplete={(result) => {
            // Handle completion
          }}
          onError={(error) => {
            // Handle errors
          }}
        />
      )
    }

#### [Props](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#props)

*   `message` - The streaming message data
*   `theme?` - Visual theme (`elegant`, `minimal`, `neobrutalism`, `terminal`)
*   `className?` - Additional CSS classes
*   `onComplete?` - Callback when streaming completes
*   `onError?` - Callback for error handling

### [CodeBlock](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#codeblock)

Syntax-highlighted code blocks with copy functionality.

    import { CodeBlock } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function CodeDisplay() {
      return (
        <CodeBlock
          code={generatedCode}
          language="typescript"
          showLineNumbers
          copyable
          theme="dark"
        />
      )
    }

#### [Props](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#props-1)

*   `code` - The code string to display
*   `language` - Programming language for syntax highlighting
*   `showLineNumbers?` - Display line numbers
*   `copyable?` - Show copy button
*   `theme?` - Color theme for syntax highlighting

### [ThinkingSection](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#thinkingsection)

Displays AI thinking process with animated indicators.

    import { ThinkingSection } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function AIThinking() {
      return (
        <ThinkingSection
          thoughts={aiThoughts}
          isVisible={showThinking}
          animated
          collapsible
        />
      )
    }

#### [Props](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#props-2)

*   `thoughts` - Array of thinking steps
*   `isVisible?` - Control visibility
*   `animated?` - Enable animations
*   `collapsible?` - Allow collapse/expand

### [TaskSection](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#tasksection)

Renders task lists and progress indicators.

    import { TaskSection } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function TaskProgress() {
      return (
        <TaskSection
          tasks={taskList}
          showProgress
          interactive
          onTaskComplete={(task) => {
            // Handle task completion
          }}
        />
      )
    }

#### [Props](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#props-3)

*   `tasks` - Array of task objects
*   `showProgress?` - Display progress bar
*   `interactive?` - Allow user interaction
*   `onTaskComplete?` - Callback for task completion

[Themes](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#themes)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

### [Built-in Themes](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#built-in-themes)

    // Elegant - Sophisticated design
    <StreamingMessage message={data} theme="elegant" />
    
    // Minimal - Clean, distraction-free
    <StreamingMessage message={data} theme="minimal" />
    
    // Neobrutalism - Bold, high-contrast
    <StreamingMessage message={data} theme="neobrutalism" />
    
    // Terminal - Developer-focused
    <StreamingMessage message={data} theme="terminal" />

### [Custom Themes](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#custom-themes)

    const customTheme = {
      primary: '#3b82f6',
      background: '#f8fafc',
      text: '#1e293b',
      accent: '#06b6d4',
      border: '#e2e8f0',
    }
    
    <StreamingMessage
      message={data}
      theme={customTheme}
    />

[Hooks](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#hooks)

---------------------------------------------------------------

### [useStreamingChat](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#usestreamingchat)

Hook for managing streaming chat state.

    import { useStreamingChat } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function ChatApp() {
      const { messages, sendMessage, isLoading, error, clearMessages } =
        useStreamingChat({
          apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
          onMessage: (message) => {
            console.log('New message:', message)
          },
        })
    
      return (
        <div>
          {messages.map((message, index) => (
            <StreamingMessage key={index} message={message} />
          ))}
    
          <button onClick={() => sendMessage('Hello!')}>Send Message</button>
        </div>
      )
    }

### [useCodeHighlight](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#usecodehighlight)

Hook for syntax highlighting with custom themes.

    import { useCodeHighlight } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    function CustomCodeBlock({ code, language }) {
      const { highlightedCode, isLoading } = useCodeHighlight({
        code,
        language,
        theme: 'github-dark',
      })
    
      if (isLoading) return <div>Loading...</div>
    
      return <pre dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: highlightedCode }} />
    }

[Styling](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#styling)

-------------------------------------------------------------------

### [CSS Custom Properties](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#css-custom-properties)

    :root {
      --v0-primary: #3b82f6;
      --v0-background: #ffffff;
      --v0-text: #1e293b;
      --v0-border: #e2e8f0;
      --v0-accent: #06b6d4;
    }
    
    .dark {
      --v0-primary: #60a5fa;
      --v0-background: #0f172a;
      --v0-text: #f1f5f9;
      --v0-border: #334155;
      --v0-accent: #22d3ee;
    }

### [Tailwind CSS Classes](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#tailwind-css-classes)

The components work seamlessly with Tailwind CSS:

    <StreamingMessage
      message={data}
      className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-4 shadow-sm"
    />

[TypeScript Support](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/react#typescript-support)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Full TypeScript support with comprehensive type definitions:

    import type {
      StreamingMessageProps,
      CodeBlockProps,
      ThinkingSectionProps,
      ChatMessage,
      StreamingState,
    } from '@v0-sdk/react'
    
    interface CustomChatProps {
      messages: ChatMessage[]
      onSendMessage: (message: string) => void
    }
    
    const CustomChat: React.FC<CustomChatProps> = ({ messages, onSendMessage }) => {
      // Component implementation
    }

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Chats

Update Chat Version Files
=========================

Copy page

Updates the source files of a specific chat version (block) manually. This allows editing generated files directly through the API.

PATCH/v1/chats/{chatId}/versions/{versionId}

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#usage)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.chats.updateVersion()
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#api-signature)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#path-parameters)

chatId: string

The unique identifier of the chat containing the version to update. Provided as a path parameter.

versionId: string

The unique identifier of the version (block) to update. Provided as a path parameter.

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#body)

files: object\[\]

Array of files to update with their new content

name: string

The full file path including extension (e.g., "components/test.tsx")

content: string

The new content for the file

locked?: boolean

Whether to lock or unlock the file to prevent AI from overwriting it during generation

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/update-version#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the version.

object: 'version'

Fixed value identifying this object as a version.

status: 'pending' | 'completed' | 'failed'

The current status of the version generation process.

demoUrl?: string

Optional URL for previewing the generated output.

screenshotUrl?: string

URL to retrieve a screenshot of this version.

createdAt: string

The date and time when the version was created, in ISO 8601 format.

updatedAt?: string

The date and time when the version was last updated, in ISO 8601 format.

files: object\[\]

A list of files that were generated or included in this version.

object: 'file'

Fixed value identifying this object as a file.

name: string

The name of the file, including its extension.

content: string

The full contents of the file as a raw string.

locked: boolean

Whether the file is locked to prevent AI from overwriting it during new version generation.

[Get Chat Version\
\
Retrieves detailed information about a specific version of a chat, including all files with their content and lock status.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/get-version)
[Resume Message\
\
Resumes processing of a previously interrupted or incomplete message in a chat. Useful for continuing generation when a message was paused or stopped.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/chats/resume)

Menu

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Hooks

Delete Hook
===========

Copy page

Deletes a webhook based on its ID. This action is irreversible.

DELETE/v1/hooks/{hookId}

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.hooks.delete({
      hookId: '123',
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete#path-parameters)

hookId: string

The ID of the webhook to delete. Provided as a path parameter.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete#response)

id: string

object: 'hook'

deleted: 'true'

[Update Hook\
\
Updates the configuration of an existing webhook, including its name, event subscriptions, or target URL.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update)
[Find Rate Limit\
\
Retrieves rate limit information for a given scope. Useful for monitoring usage limits and avoiding throttling.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/rate-limits/find)

Menu

Account
=======

Copy page

Manage your account and billing information.

You can manage your account from the settings page. To access this, click your avatar in the top right corner of the interface and select **Settings**.

[Billing](https://v0.app/docs/account#billing)

-----------------------------------------------

You can view your billing information in the settings. This includes your current plan, payment methods, and invoices. Viewing invoices will take you to your Vercel dashboard.

[Learn more about pricing](https://v0.app/docs/pricing)

[Cancelling your subscription](https://v0.app/docs/account#cancelling-your-subscription)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can cancel your subscription at any time. To do this:

1.  Ensure you have selected the scope whose subscription you want to cancel using the dropdown located at the top left of the page
2.  Click your avatar in the top right corner of the interface
3.  Click on **Settings**
4.  Click on **Billing**
5.  In the **Current Plan** section, click on **Cancel Plan**

This will move your account to the free plan at the end of your current billing period.

[Account recovery](https://v0.app/docs/account#account-recovery)

-----------------------------------------------------------------

Once a account or team has been confirmed for deletion, the deletion process cannot be stopped nor the account recovered. If you wish to reuse , you will need to wait 7 days to sign up with the same email address.

For chats, once a chat is deleted, it will be stored in your [chat archive](https://v0.app/chat/archive)
. Chats will exist in your archive for 30 days, during which they can be restored before being permanently deleted.

[Templates\
\
Share your v0 creations with the community by publishing them as templates. Templates appear in your public profile and can be forked by other users.](https://v0.app/docs/templates)
[Community\
\
Manage your shared community projects.](https://v0.app/docs/community)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Integrations

Find Vercel Projects
====================

Copy page

Retrieves a list of Vercel projects linked to your integration. Useful for associating chats, deployments, or hooks with specific Vercel projects.

GET/v1/integrations/vercel/projects

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.find#usage)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.integrations.vercel.projects.find()
    
    console.log(result)

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.find#response)

object: 'list'

data: object\[\]

id?: string

A unique identifier for the linked Vercel project.

object?: 'vercel\_project'

Fixed value identifying this object as a Vercel project.

name?: string

The name of the Vercel project.

[Create Vercel Project\
\
Links a Vercel project to an existing v0 project. Enables Vercel-related features and deployment integration within the v0 workspace.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/integrations/integrations.vercel.projects.create)
[Find Hooks\
\
Retrieves a list of existing hooks in your workspace. Useful for managing active webhooks tied to chat events or deployments.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/find)

v0 Platform API/Packages

@v0-sdk/ai-tools
================

Copy page

AI SDK tools for the v0 Platform API

AI SDK tools that enable autonomous agents to interact with the v0 Platform API. Build intelligent workflows that can create projects, manage chats, handle deployments, and more.

[Installation](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#installation)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    npm install @v0-sdk/ai-tools ai
    # or
    pnpm add @v0-sdk/ai-tools ai
    # or
    yarn add @v0-sdk/ai-tools ai

[Quick Start](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#quick-start)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    import { generateText } from 'ai'
    import { v0Tools } from '@v0-sdk/ai-tools'
    
    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Create a new React todo app project',
      tools: v0Tools({
        apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
      }),
    })
    
    console.log(result.text)

[Tool Categories](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#tool-categories)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [All Tools (High Context)](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#all-tools-high-context)

Use all available tools for maximum capability:

    import { v0Tools } from '@v0-sdk/ai-tools'
    
    const tools = v0Tools({
      apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
    })
    
    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Build a complete web app with deployment',
      tools,
    })

⚠️ **Note**: Includes 20+ tools which adds significant context to AI calls.

### [Selective Tools (Recommended)](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#selective-tools-recommended)

Choose specific tool categories for better performance:

    import { v0ToolsByCategory } from '@v0-sdk/ai-tools'
    
    const tools = v0ToolsByCategory({
      apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
    })
    
    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Create a new project and start a chat',
      tools: {
        ...tools.project, // Project management tools
        ...tools.chat, // Chat tools
      },
    })

[Available Tool Categories](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#available-tool-categories)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Chat Tools](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#chat-tools)

    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Create a chat about building a landing page',
      tools: tools.chat,
    })

**Available tools:**

*   `createChat` - Create new chats
*   `sendMessage` - Send messages to chats
*   `getChat` - Retrieve chat details
*   `findChats` - List user chats
*   `deleteChat` - Remove chats

### [Project Tools](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#project-tools)

    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Create a new project called "My Portfolio"',
      tools: tools.project,
    })

**Available tools:**

*   `createProject` - Create new projects
*   `getProject` - Get project details
*   `findProjects` - List projects
*   `updateProject` - Modify projects
*   `deleteProject` - Remove projects

### [Deployment Tools](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#deployment-tools)

    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Deploy the project and check its status',
      tools: tools.deployment,
    })

**Available tools:**

*   `createDeployment` - Deploy projects
*   `getDeployment` - Check deployment status
*   `findDeployments` - List deployments
*   `getDeploymentLogs` - View deployment logs
*   `getDeploymentErrors` - Check for errors

### [User Tools](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#user-tools)

    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Check my account information and billing status',
      tools: tools.user,
    })

**Available tools:**

*   `getUser` - Get user information
*   `getUserBilling` - Check billing details
*   `getUserPlan` - View subscription plan
*   `getUserScopes` - Check permissions

### [Hook Tools](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#hook-tools)

    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Set up a webhook for deployment notifications',
      tools: tools.hook,
    })

**Available tools:**

*   `createHook` - Create webhooks
*   `getHook` - Get webhook details
*   `findHooks` - List webhooks
*   `updateHook` - Modify webhooks
*   `deleteHook` - Remove webhooks

[Agent Patterns](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#agent-patterns)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Multi-Step Agent](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#multi-step-agent)

    import { generateText, stopWhen, stepCountIs } from 'ai'
    
    const result = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Build and deploy a complete todo app',
      tools: {
        ...tools.project,
        ...tools.chat,
        ...tools.deployment,
      },
      stopWhen: stepCountIs(5), // Limit execution steps
    })

### [Sequential Processing](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#sequential-processing)

    // Step 1: Create project
    const projectResult = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Create a new project for a todo app',
      tools: tools.project,
    })
    
    // Step 2: Start development chat
    const chatResult = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: `Create a chat for project ${projectResult.toolResults[0].result.id}`,
      tools: tools.chat,
    })
    
    // Step 3: Deploy when ready
    const deployResult = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: 'Deploy the completed project',
      tools: tools.deployment,
    })

### [Routing Agent](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#routing-agent)

    import { generateText } from 'ai'
    
    const routingResult = await generateText({
      model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
      prompt: userRequest,
      tools: {
        routeToProject: tool({
          description: 'Route to project management',
          parameters: z.object({
            action: z.string(),
          }),
        }),
        routeToChat: tool({
          description: 'Route to chat management',
          parameters: z.object({
            action: z.string(),
          }),
        }),
      },
    })
    
    // Use appropriate tools based on routing
    const tools =
      routingResult.toolResults[0].toolName === 'routeToProject'
        ? tools.project
        : tools.chat

### [Parallel Processing](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#parallel-processing)

    const [projectResult, userResult] = await Promise.all([\
      generateText({\
        model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),\
        prompt: 'Analyze my projects',\
        tools: tools.project,\
      }),\
      generateText({\
        model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),\
        prompt: 'Check my account status',\
        tools: tools.user,\
      }),\
    ])

[Configuration](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#configuration)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Environment Variables](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#environment-variables)

    V0_API_KEY=your_v0_api_key_here
    AI_GATEWAY_API_KEY=your_ai_gateway_api_key_here

### [Custom Configuration](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#custom-configuration)

    const tools = v0ToolsByCategory({
      apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
      baseURL: 'https://api.v0.dev/v1', // Optional
      timeout: 30000, // Optional
    })

[Error Handling](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#error-handling)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    try {
      const result = await generateText({
        model: openai('gpt-4o-mini'),
        prompt: 'Create a project',
        tools: tools.project,
      })
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.name === 'V0Error') {
        console.error('v0 API error:', error.message)
      } else if (error.name === 'AIError') {
        console.error('AI SDK error:', error.message)
      } else {
        console.error('Unexpected error:', error)
      }
    }

[Best Practices](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#best-practices)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Use selective tools** - Only include categories you need
2.  **Set step limits** - Use `stopWhen` to control execution
3.  **Handle errors** - Wrap calls in try-catch blocks
4.  **Monitor usage** - Track API calls and costs
5.  **Test incrementally** - Start with simple workflows

[Requirements](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/ai-tools#requirements)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 22+
*   AI SDK 5.0+
*   v0 API key from [v0.dev](https://v0.dev/chat/settings/keys)

v0 Platform API/Packages

create-v0-sdk-app
=================

Copy page

Create v0 SDK-powered apps with one command

A command-line tool for quickly scaffolding new applications powered by the v0 SDK. Get started with pre-built templates and examples.

[Installation](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#installation)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No installation required! Use with `npx`:

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-app

Or install globally:

    npm install -g create-v0-sdk-app
    create-v0-sdk-app my-app

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#usage)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Interactive Mode](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#interactive-mode)

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest

The CLI will prompt you for:

*   **Project name**: Your app's directory name
*   **Template**: Choose from available templates
*   **Package manager**: npm, pnpm, or yarn

### [Direct Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#direct-usage)

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-app --template v0-clone

[Available Templates](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#available-templates)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [v0 Clone](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#v0-clone)

A full-featured replica of v0.dev with authentication and multi-tenant support.

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-app --template v0-clone

**Features:**

*   User authentication (NextAuth.js)
*   Multi-tenant architecture
*   PostgreSQL database with Drizzle ORM
*   Real-time streaming
*   Rate limiting

### [Classic v0](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#classic-v0)

The iconic v0.dev interface with three-generation workflow.

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-app --template classic-v0

**Features:**

*   Classic v0 UI/UX
*   Multiple generations (A, B, C)
*   shadcn/ui components
*   Next.js 15 with App Router

### [AI Tools Example](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#ai-tools-example)

Demonstrates AI SDK integration with v0 tools.

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-app --template ai-tools-example

**Features:**

*   AI SDK integration
*   v0 tools for autonomous agents
*   Multiple agent patterns
*   TypeScript examples

[Command Options](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#command-options)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    create-v0-sdk-app [project-name] [options]

### [Options](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#options)

*   `--template <name>` - Specify template (v0-clone, classic-v0, ai-tools-example)
*   `--package-manager <pm>` - Choose package manager (npm, pnpm, yarn)
*   `--help` - Show help information
*   `--version` - Show version number

[Examples](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#examples)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Create a v0 clone](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#create-a-v0-clone)

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-v0-clone --template v0-clone
    cd my-v0-clone

Set up environment variables:

    cp .env.example .env
    # Edit .env with your API keys

Install dependencies and start:

    pnpm install
    pnpm db:migrate  # For v0-clone template
    pnpm dev

### [Create a classic v0 interface](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#create-a-classic-v0-interface)

    npx create-v0-sdk-app@latest my-classic-app --template classic-v0
    cd my-classic-app
    pnpm install
    pnpm dev

[Post-Creation Steps](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#post-creation-steps)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After creating your app:

1.  **Set up environment variables**:
    
        cp .env.example .env
        # Add your V0_API_KEY
    
2.  **Install dependencies**:
    
        pnpm install
    
3.  **Database setup** (for v0-clone template):
    
        pnpm db:migrate
    
4.  **Start development server**:
    
        pnpm dev
    

[Template Structure](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#template-structure)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each template includes:

*   **Complete source code** - Ready-to-run application
*   **Documentation** - Setup and usage instructions
*   **Environment examples** - `.env.example` files
*   **Package configuration** - Optimized `package.json`
*   **TypeScript config** - Proper TypeScript setup

[Customization](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#customization)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After creation, you can:

*   **Modify components** - All source code is yours to customize
*   **Add features** - Extend with additional v0 SDK capabilities
*   **Change styling** - Update themes and design systems
*   **Deploy** - Ready for deployment to Vercel, Netlify, etc.

[Requirements](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#requirements)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 22+
*   pnpm 9+ (recommended)
*   v0 API key from [v0.dev](https://v0.dev/chat/settings/keys)
    

[Links](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/create-v0-sdk-app#links)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [GitHub Repository](https://github.com/vercel/v0-sdk/tree/main/packages/create-v0-sdk-app)
    
*   [npm Package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/create-v0-sdk-app)
    
*   [Template Examples](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/examples)

v0 Platform API/Packages

v0-sdk
======

Copy page

TypeScript SDK for the v0 Platform API

The core TypeScript SDK for interacting with the v0 Platform API. Provides type-safe methods for creating chats, managing projects, handling deployments, and more.

[Installation](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#installation)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    npm install v0-sdk
    # or
    pnpm add v0-sdk
    # or
    yarn add v0-sdk

[Quick Start](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#quick-start)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

    import { V0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const v0 = new V0({
      apiKey: process.env.V0_API_KEY,
    })
    
    // Create a new chat
    const chat = await v0.chats.create({
      message: 'Create a todo app with React',
    })
    
    console.log(chat.id)

[Features](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#features)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Type-safe API**: Full TypeScript support with comprehensive type definitions
*   **Complete Coverage**: Access all v0 Platform API endpoints
*   **Modern Architecture**: Built with modern JavaScript/TypeScript patterns
*   **Error Handling**: Comprehensive error handling and validation
*   **Streaming Support**: Real-time streaming for chat responses

[Core APIs](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#core-apis)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Chats](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#chats)

    // Create a chat
    const chat = await v0.chats.create({
      message: 'Build a landing page',
    })
    
    // Send a message
    const response = await v0.chats.sendMessage(chat.id, {
      message: 'Add a contact form',
    })
    
    // Get chat history
    const chatData = await v0.chats.getById(chat.id)

### [Projects](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#projects)

    // Create a project
    const project = await v0.projects.create({
      name: 'My App',
    })
    
    // Get project details
    const projectData = await v0.projects.getById(project.id)
    
    // List all projects
    const projects = await v0.projects.find()

### [Deployments](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#deployments)

    // Create a deployment
    const deployment = await v0.deployments.create({
      projectId: project.id,
      chatId: chat.id,
      versionId: chat.latestVersion.id,
    })
    
    // Get deployment status
    const deploymentData = await v0.deployments.getById(deployment.id)
    
    // Get deployment logs
    const logs = await v0.deployments.findLogs(deployment.id)

### [User & Account](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#user--account)

    // Get user information
    const user = await v0.user.get()
    
    // Get billing information
    const billing = await v0.user.getBilling()
    
    // Get current plan
    const plan = await v0.user.getPlan()

[Configuration](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#configuration)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Environment Variables](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#environment-variables)

    V0_API_KEY=your_api_key_here
    V0_API_URL=https://api.v0.dev/v1  # Optional, defaults to production

### [Client Options](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#client-options)

    const v0 = new V0({
      apiKey: 'your-api-key',
      baseURL: 'https://api.v0.dev/v1', // Optional
      timeout: 30000, // Optional, in milliseconds
      maxRetries: 3, // Optional
    })

[Error Handling](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#error-handling)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    import { V0Error } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    try {
      const chat = await v0.chats.create({
        message: 'Create an app',
      })
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof V0Error) {
        console.error('API Error:', error.message)
        console.error('Status:', error.status)
        console.error('Code:', error.code)
      } else {
        console.error('Unexpected error:', error)
      }
    }

[Requirements](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#requirements)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 22+
*   TypeScript 5.0+ (for TypeScript projects)

[Links](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/packages/v0-sdk#links)

----------------------------------------------------------------

*   [npm Package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/v0-sdk)
    
*   [API Reference](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Hooks

Update Hook
===========

Copy page

Updates the configuration of an existing webhook, including its name, event subscriptions, or target URL.

PATCH/v1/hooks/{hookId}

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.hooks.update({
      hookId: '123',
      name: 'My Updated Hook',
      events: ['chat.created', 'message.created'],
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#path-parameters)

hookId: string

The ID of the webhook to update. Provided as a path parameter.

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#body)

name?: string

A new name for the hook.

events?: 'chat.created' | 'chat.updated' | 'chat.deleted' | 'message.created' | 'message.updated' | 'message.deleted' | 'message.finished'\[\]

Updated list of event types to subscribe to.

url?: string

A new URL to send webhook payloads to.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/update#response)

id: string

A unique identifier for the webhook.

object: 'hook'

Fixed value identifying this object as a webhook.

name: string

A user-defined name to label the webhook.

events: 'chat.created' | 'chat.updated' | 'chat.deleted' | 'message.created' | 'message.updated' | 'message.deleted' | 'message.finished'\[\]

List of event types this webhook is subscribed to.

chatId?: string

Optional ID of the chat that this webhook is scoped to.

url: string

Target URL that receives event payloads for this webhook.

[Get Hook\
\
Retrieves the details of a specific webhook using its ID.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/get-by-id)
[Delete Hook\
\
Deletes a webhook based on its ID. This action is irreversible.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/hooks/delete)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Projects

Assign Project to Chat
======================

Copy page

Links an existing v0 project to a specific chat. Helps group conversations under a shared project context.

POST/v1/projects/{projectId}/assign

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#usage)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.projects.assign({
      projectId: '123',
      chatId: '123',
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#api-signature)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#path-parameters)

projectId: string

The ID of the project to assign.

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#body)

chatId: string

The ID of the chat to assign the project to.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign#response)

object: 'project'

id: string

assigned: 'true'

[Update Project\
\
Updates the metadata of an existing project using its \`projectId\`. Supports changes to the project name and privacy setting.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/update)
[Create Environment Variables\
\
Creates new environment variables for a given project. This endpoint will fail if any of the specified environment variable keys already exist, unless upsert is set to true.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Projects

Delete Project
==============

Copy page

Deletes a specific project based on the provided projectId. This operation marks the project as deleted and is irreversible.

DELETE/v1/projects/{projectId}

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete#usage)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.projects.delete({
      projectId: 'abcd1234',
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete#api-signature)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete#path-parameters)

projectId: string

The unique identifier of the project to delete. This must be passed as a path parameter in the URL.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete#response)

id: string

The unique identifier of the deleted project.

object: 'project'

Fixed value identifying this object as a project.

deleted: 'true'

Confirmation that the project has been deleted.

[Create Environment Variables\
\
Creates new environment variables for a given project. This endpoint will fail if any of the specified environment variable keys already exist, unless upsert is set to true.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars)
[Delete Environment Variables\
\
Deletes multiple environment variables for a given project by their IDs.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars)

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Projects

Delete Environment Variables
============================

Copy page

Deletes multiple environment variables for a given project by their IDs.

POST/v1/projects/{projectId}/env-vars/delete

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.projects.deleteEnvVars({
      projectId: 'project_abc123',
      environmentVariableIds: ['env_def456', 'env_ghi789'],
    })
    
    console.log(result)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#path-parameters)

projectId: string

The unique identifier of the project whose environment variables should be deleted.

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#body)

environmentVariableIds: string\[\]

An array of environment variable IDs to delete.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete-env-vars#response)

object: 'list'

data: object\[\]

id: string

object: 'environment\_variable'

deleted: 'true'

[Delete Project\
\
Deletes a specific project based on the provided projectId. This operation marks the project as deleted and is irreversible.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete)
[Find Environment Variables\
\
Retrieves all environment variables for a given project.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/find-env-vars)

Menu

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Projects

Create Environment Variables
============================

Copy page

Creates new environment variables for a given project. This endpoint will fail if any of the specified environment variable keys already exist, unless upsert is set to true.

POST/v1/projects/{projectId}/env-vars

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#usage)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    // Create new environment variables (will fail if keys already exist)
    const result = await v0.projects.createEnvVars({
      projectId: 'project_abc123',
      environmentVariables: [\
        {\
          key: 'DATABASE_URL',\
          value: 'postgresql://user:pass@host:5432/db',\
        },\
        {\
          key: 'API_SECRET_KEY',\
          value: 'sk_1234567890abcdef',\
        },\
      ],
    })
    
    console.log(result)
    
    // Upsert environment variables (will overwrite existing values)
    const upsertResult = await v0.projects.createEnvVars({
      projectId: 'project_abc123',
      upsert: true,
      environmentVariables: [\
        {\
          key: 'DATABASE_URL',\
          value: 'postgresql://newuser:newpass@newhost:5432/newdb',\
        },\
      ],
    })
    
    console.log(upsertResult)

[API Signature](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#api-signature)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Request](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#request)

#### [Path Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#path-parameters)

projectId: string

The unique identifier of the project where environment variables should be created.

#### [Query Parameters](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#query-parameters)

decrypted?: 'true' | 'false'

Whether to return decrypted values. Defaults to false (encrypted).

#### [Body](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#body)

environmentVariables: object\[\]

An array of environment variables to create with key and value fields.

key: string

The name of the environment variable.

value: string

The value of the environment variable.

upsert?: boolean

Whether to overwrite existing environment variables with the same keys. Defaults to false.

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create-env-vars#response)

object: 'list'

data: object\[\]

id?: string

A unique identifier for the environment variable.

object?: 'environment\_variable'

The object type.

key?: string

The name of the environment variable.

value?: string

The value of the environment variable.

decrypted?: boolean

Whether the value is decrypted or encrypted.

createdAt?: number

The timestamp when the environment variable was created.

updatedAt?: number

The timestamp when the environment variable was last updated.

[Assign Project to Chat\
\
Links an existing v0 project to a specific chat. Helps group conversations under a shared project context.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/assign)
[Delete Project\
\
Deletes a specific project based on the provided projectId. This operation marks the project as deleted and is irreversible.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/delete)

Menu

v0 Platform API/API Reference/Projects

Find Projects
=============

Copy page

Returns a list of all v0 projects in your workspace. Useful for browsing or managing projects across different chats or use cases.

GET/v1/projects

[Usage](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/find#usage)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript Example

TypeScriptcURL

    import { v0 } from 'v0-sdk'
    
    const result = await v0.projects.find()
    
    console.log(result)

### [Response](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/find#response)

object: 'list'

data: object\[\]

id?: string

A unique identifier for the project.

object?: 'project'

Fixed value identifying this object as a project.

name?: string

The name of the project as defined by the user.

privacy?: 'private' | 'team'

The privacy setting for the project - either private or team.

vercelProjectId?: string

Optional ID of the linked Vercel project, if connected.

createdAt?: string

The ISO timestamp representing when the project was created.

updatedAt?: string

The ISO timestamp of the most recent update, if available.

apiUrl?: string

The API endpoint URL for accessing this project programmatically.

webUrl?: string

The web URL where the project can be viewed or managed.

[Create Project\
\
Creates a new v0 project with an optional description, icon, environment variables, and instructions. Projects help organize chats and manage context.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/create)
[Get Project by ID\
\
Retrieves the details of a specific v0 project by its ID.](https://v0.app/docs/api/platform/reference/projects/get-by-id)
